about_this_resource_text: <h2 class="subhead">Description</h2> <p>In this video, which
  plays from the 00:23:28 to the end, Dr. Jeremy Kepner leads the class to explore
  the AI data architecture in data processing.</p> <p><strong>Instructor:</strong>
  Jeremy Kepner</p>

  <span m="2068040">AI,</span> <span m="2069179">this</span> <span m="2069510">pipeline</span>
  <span m="2070320">represents,</span> <span m="2071610">pretty</span> <span m="2072000">much,</span>
  <span m="2072420">what</span> <span m="2072659">most</span> <span m="2073080">applications</span>
  <span m="2073830">are</span> <span m="2073889">doing.</span> <span m="2074219">It's</span>
  <span m="2074370">not</span> <span m="2074580">that</span> <span m="2074699">any</span>
  <span m="2074969">application</span> <span m="2075610">does</span> <span m="2075900">all</span>
  <span m="2076170">of</span> <span m="2076290">that,</span> <span m="2076989">but</span>
  <span m="2077040">most</span> <span m="2077409">of</span> <span m="2077460">the</span>
  <span m="2077550">steps</span> <span m="2077940">in</span> <span m="2078030">an</span>
  <span m="2078139">application</span> <span m="2078780">fall</span> <span m="2079199">into</span>
  <span m="2079500">this</span> <span m="2079770">pipeline.</span></p><p><span m="2080610">Basically,</span>
  <span m="2081060">you</span> <span m="2081179">have</span> <span m="2081429">raw</span>

  <span m="2095940">all</span> <span m="2096150">the</span> <span m="2096239">files,</span>

  <span m="2280170">tabular</span> <span m="2280710">data.</span></p><p><span m="2282130">And</span>
  <span m="2282870">because</span> <span m="2283350">of</span> <span m="2283470">this,</span>
  <span m="2283770">tabular</span> <span m="2284280">data</span> <span m="2284640">is</span>
  <span m="2284910">compatible</span> <span m="2285660">with</span> <span m="2285900">almost</span>
  <span m="2286380">every</span> <span m="2286800">data</span> <span m="2287220">analysis</span>
  <span m="2288360">software</span> <span m="2288900">on</span> <span m="2289110">earth.</span>
  <span m="2289800">If</span> <span m="2289980">I</span> <span m="2290110">make</span>
  <span m="2290310">data</span> <span m="2290580">analysis</span> <span m="2290980">software</span>
  <span m="2291400">and it</span> <span m="2291490">can't</span> <span m="2291810">read</span>
  <span m="2292440">tables</span> <span m="2292980">or</span> <span m="2293040">write</span>
  <span m="2293340">out</span> <span m="2293490">tables,</span> <span m="2293940">it's</span>
  <span m="2294060">going</span> <span m="2294170">to</span> <span m="2294240">have</span>
  <span m="2294390">a</span> <span m="2294450">very</span> <span m="2294780">small</span>
  <span m="2295050">market</span> <span m="2295470">share.</span> <span m="2296010">And</span>
  <span m="2296100">this</span> <span m="2296310">is</span> <span m="2296470">just</span>
  <span m="2296640">an</span> <span m="2296760">example</span> <span m="2297420">of</span>
  <span m="2297680">some</span> <span m="2298010">of</span> <span m="2298190">the</span>
  <span m="2299690">software</span> <span m="2300230">out</span> <span m="2300530">there</span>
  <span m="2300800">that</span> <span m="2300980">is</span> <span m="2301190">designed</span>
  <span m="2301610">to</span> <span m="2301700">use</span> <span m="2301940">tables.</span>
  <span m="2302420">So</span> <span m="2302690">whether</span> <span m="2302960">it</span>
  <span m="2303020">be</span> <span m="2303200">spreadsheets</span> <span m="2304340">or</span>
  <span m="2304460">databases</span> <span m="2305520">or</span> <span m="2305660">the</span>
  <span m="2305780">neural</span> <span m="2306080">network</span> <span m="2306410">packages</span>
  <span m="2307040">that</span> <span m="2307190">we've</span> <span m="2307370">already</span>
  <span m="2307670">looked</span> <span m="2307940">at,</span> <span m="2308480">various</span>
  <span m="2308870">languages</span> <span m="2309440">and</span> <span m="2309530">libraries,</span>
  <span m="2310470">and</span> <span m="2310520">even</span> <span m="2310880">things</span>
  <span m="2311210">that</span> <span m="2311360">you</span> <span m="2311450">wouldn't</span>
  <span m="2311720">think</span> <span m="2312080">are</span> <span m="2312200">tabular</span>
  <span m="2312770">like</span> <span m="2313280">hierarchical</span> <span m="2313790">file</span>
  <span m="2314120">formats,</span> <span m="2314510">like</span> <span m="2314690">JSON</span>
  <span m="2315170">and</span> <span m="2315260">XML,</span> <span m="2316010">can</span>
  <span m="2316220">actually</span> <span m="2316790">be</span> <span m="2316940">made</span>
  <span m="2317210">compatible</span> <span m="2318290">with</span> <span m="2318680">a</span>
  <span m="2318770">tablet</span> <span m="2319190">format.</span></p><p><span m="2320130">So</span>
  <span m="2320150">I'm</span> <span m="2320210">just</span> <span m="2320330">going</span>
  <span m="2320400">to</span> <span m="2320480">walk</span> <span m="2321350">through</span>
  <span m="2321710">these</span> <span m="2322040">in a</span> <span m="2322130">little</span>
  <span m="2322310">more</span> <span m="2322730">detail.</span> <span m="2324450">So</span>
  <span m="2324920">of</span> <span m="2325010">course,</span> <span m="2325310">our</span>
  <span m="2325400">favorite</span> <span m="2325860">is</span> <span m="2326000">spreadsheets.</span>
  <span m="2327200">Here's</span> <span m="2327500">an</span> <span m="2327560">example</span>
  <span m="2328070">of</span> <span m="2328160">a</span> <span m="2328250">spreadsheet,</span>
  <span m="2329450">on</span> <span m="2329690">the</span> <span m="2329780">left.</span>
  <span m="2330380">And</span> <span m="2330500">what's</span> <span m="2330740">great</span>
  <span m="2330980">about</span> <span m="2331250">it</span> <span m="2331310">is</span>
  <span m="2331460">that</span> <span m="2331610">I</span> <span m="2331700">have</span>
  <span m="2332600">four</span> <span m="2332960">different</span> <span m="2333350">types</span>
  <span m="2333770">of</span> <span m="2333890">data</span> <span m="2334640">that
  are</span> <span m="2334970">very,</span> <span m="2335670">very</span> <span m="2335810">different,</span>
  <span m="2336170">and</span> <span m="2336290">you</span> <span m="2336380">can</span>
  <span m="2336530">all</span> <span m="2336830">look</span> <span m="2337070">at</span>
  <span m="2337190">them</span> <span m="2337460">and</span> <span m="2337580">sort</span>
  <span m="2337790">of</span> <span m="2337850">get</span> <span m="2338030">a</span>
  <span m="2338090">sense</span> <span m="2338420">of</span> <span m="2338540">what</span>
  <span m="2338660">they</span> <span m="2338820">are.</span> <span m="2339800">And</span>
  <span m="2339920">that</span> <span m="2340100">just</span> <span m="2340280">shows</span>
  <span m="2340610">how</span> <span m="2340820">flexible</span> <span m="2342050">this</span>
  <span m="2342230">tabular</span> <span m="2342860">spreadsheet</span> <span m="2343490">form</span>
  <span m="2344000">is,</span> <span m="2344630">is</span> <span m="2344810">that</span>
  <span m="2345920">we</span> <span m="2346010">can</span> <span m="2346160">handle</span>
  <span m="2346490">really,</span> <span m="2346980">really</span> <span m="2347120">diverse</span>
  <span m="2347510">types</span> <span m="2347810">of</span> <span m="2347900">data</span>
  <span m="2348380">in</span> <span m="2348470">a</span> <span m="2348530">way</span>
  <span m="2348680">that's</span> <span m="2348920">intuitive</span> <span m="2349550">to</span>
  <span m="2349760">us.</span></p><p><span m="2350660">Some</span> <span m="2350900">of</span>
  <span m="2350960">the</span> <span m="2351050">biggest</span> <span m="2351440">pieces</span>
  <span m="2351890">of</span> <span m="2351950">software</span> <span m="2352460">that</span>
  <span m="2352640">are</span> <span m="2353110">huge</span> <span m="2353540">that</span>
  <span m="2353870">implement</span> <span m="2354320">this</span> <span m="2354530">are</span>
  <span m="2354620">Microsoft</span> <span m="2355160">Excel,</span> <span m="2356030">Google</span>
  <span m="2356330">Sheets,</span> <span m="2357170">Apple</span> <span m="2357470">Numbers.</span>
  <span m="2358490">It's</span> <span m="2358700">used</span> <span m="2359000">by</span>
  <span m="2359300">about</span> <span m="2359600">100</span> <span m="2360020">million</span>
  <span m="2360410">people</span> <span m="2361010">every</span> <span m="2361310">day.</span>
  <span m="2362480">And</span> <span m="2362660">so,</span> <span m="2363080">this</span>
  <span m="2363410">is</span> <span m="2363560">the</span> <span m="2363680">most</span>
  <span m="2363890">popular</span> <span m="2364970">tool</span> <span m="2365330">for</span>
  <span m="2365510">using</span> <span m="2365870">data</span> <span m="2366170">analysis,</span>
  <span m="2367220">and</span> <span m="2367580">there's</span> <span m="2367790">a</span>
  <span m="2367850">good</span> <span m="2368090">reason</span> <span m="2368450">for</span>
  <span m="2368790">it.</span> <span m="2369160">And</span> <span m="2369740">thinking</span>
  <span m="2370160">of</span> <span m="2370280">things</span> <span m="2370580">in</span>
  <span m="2370700">a</span> <span m="2370760">tabular</span> <span m="2371240">format</span>
  <span m="2372150">so</span> <span m="2372270">they</span> <span m="2372410">can</span>
  <span m="2372560">be</span> <span m="2372680">pulled</span> <span m="2373040">into</span>
  <span m="2373250">this</span> <span m="2373730">really</span> <span m="2374090">makes</span>
  <span m="2374390">communication</span> <span m="2375320">a</span> <span m="2375380">lot</span>
  <span m="2375710">easier.</span> <span m="2376350">And</span> <span m="2376430">so</span>
  <span m="2376730">again,</span> <span m="2377120">just</span> <span m="2377330">sort
  of</span> <span m="2377480">hammering</span> <span m="2377900">home</span> <span
  m="2378110">this</span> <span m="2378710">element</span> <span m="2379100">of</span>
  <span m="2379220">tables.</span></p><p><span m="2380150">Within</span> <span m="2380540">that,</span>
  <span m="2380900">there's</span> <span m="2381080">specific</span> <span m="2381860">formats</span>
  <span m="2382400">that</span> <span m="2382680">we have</span> <span m="2382790">found</span>
  <span m="2383120">to</span> <span m="2383180">be</span> <span m="2383330">very</span>
  <span m="2383570">popular.</span> <span m="2384660">So</span> <span m="2384800">CSV</span>
  <span m="2385550">and</span> <span m="2385640">TSV</span> <span m="2386270">are</span>
  <span m="2386420">just</span> <span m="2387500">non-proprietary,</span> <span m="2389070">plain</span>
  <span m="2389690">text</span> <span m="2390560">ways</span> <span m="2391100">of</span>
  <span m="2391220">organizing</span> <span m="2391970">data.</span> <span m="2392350">We</span>
  <span m="2392510">highly</span> <span m="2392990">encourage</span> <span m="2393470">people</span>
  <span m="2393740">to</span> <span m="2393830">use</span> <span m="2394070">them</span>
  <span m="2394220">because</span> <span m="2394460">then</span> <span m="2394640">it</span>
  <span m="2394730">can</span> <span m="2394880">be</span> <span m="2395000">used</span>
  <span m="2395270">by</span> <span m="2395900">any</span> <span m="2396170">tool.</span>
  <span m="2396930">CSV</span> <span m="2397730">just</span> <span m="2397940">stands</span>
  <span m="2398300">for</span> <span m="2398450">comma</span> <span m="2398840">separated</span>
  <span m="2399410">values.</span> <span m="2399920">It's</span> <span m="2400070">usually</span>
  <span m="2400430">filename.csv</span> <span m="2401940">in</span> <span m="2402080">lower</span>
  <span m="2402350">case</span> <span m="2402690">or</span> <span m="2402780">filename.CSV</span>
  <span m="2403940">in</span> <span m="2404070">upper</span> <span m="2404320">case.</span>
  <span m="2405050">And</span> <span m="2405260">all</span> <span m="2405530">it</span>
  <span m="2405620">means</span> <span m="2406040">is</span> <span m="2406220">that</span>
  <span m="2407120">the</span> <span m="2407240">columns--</span> <span m="2408530">So</span>
  <span m="2408740">each</span> <span m="2409340">row</span> <span m="2410180">is</span>
  <span m="2410360">terminated</span> <span m="2410930">by</span> <span m="2411110">a</span>
  <span m="2411140">new</span> <span m="2411380">line,</span> <span m="2411800">and</span>
  <span m="2411950">within</span> <span m="2412250">each</span> <span m="2412460">row</span>
  <span m="2412700">the</span> <span m="2412820">columns</span> <span m="2413240">are</span>
  <span m="2413330">separated</span> <span m="2413840">by</span> <span m="2414020">a</span>
  <span m="2414080">comma.</span> <span m="2414920">That's</span> <span m="2415250">all</span>
  <span m="2415520">that</span> <span m="2415730">means.</span></p><p><span m="2417110">We</span>
  <span m="2417350">tend</span> <span m="2417710">to</span> <span m="2417890">encourage</span>
  <span m="2418490">people</span> <span m="2418910">to</span> <span m="2419090">use</span>
  <span m="2419420">TSV,</span> <span m="2420140">which</span> <span m="2420350">stands</span>
  <span m="2420650">for</span> <span m="2420800">tab</span> <span m="2421580">separated</span>
  <span m="2422150">values,</span> <span m="2422960">because</span> <span m="2423470">we</span>
  <span m="2423620">can</span> <span m="2423740">replace</span> <span m="2424280">the</span>
  <span m="2424400">comma</span> <span m="2424910">with</span> <span m="2425120">a</span>
  <span m="2425180">tab.</span> <span m="2426200">And</span> <span m="2426350">that</span>
  <span m="2426560">allows</span> <span m="2426950">us</span> <span m="2427070">to</span>
  <span m="2427220">write</span> <span m="2427550">higher</span> <span m="2427970">performance</span>
  <span m="2429110">readers</span> <span m="2429560">and</span> <span m="2429680">writers.</span>
  <span m="2430580">Because</span> <span m="2431870">it</span> <span m="2431990">is</span>
  <span m="2432110">not</span> <span m="2432440">uncommon</span> <span m="2433130">to</span>
  <span m="2433280">have</span> <span m="2433640">a</span> <span m="2433730">comma</span>
  <span m="2434540">within</span> <span m="2434900">a</span> <span m="2434960">value,</span>
  <span m="2435830">and</span> <span m="2435980">so</span> <span m="2436190">it</span>
  <span m="2436280">makes</span> <span m="2436520">it</span> <span m="2436610">very</span>
  <span m="2436910">difficult</span> <span m="2437870">to</span> <span m="2438320">write</span>
  <span m="2438590">parsers</span> <span m="2439160">that</span> <span m="2439310">can</span>
  <span m="2439490">do</span> <span m="2439670">that</span> <span m="2439880">fast.</span>
  <span m="2441170">But</span> <span m="2441380">it's</span> <span m="2441590">OK</span>
  <span m="2442070">to</span> <span m="2442160">say</span> <span m="2442940">to</span>
  <span m="2443450">a</span> <span m="2443480">person</span> <span m="2443870">generating</span>
  <span m="2444440">data,</span> <span m="2444810">if</span> <span m="2444830">you</span>
  <span m="2444950">put</span> <span m="2445220">a</span> <span m="2445310">tab</span>
  <span m="2446330">inside</span> <span m="2447470">a</span> <span m="2447570">value</span>
  <span m="2448880">that's</span> <span m="2449180">a</span> <span m="2449240">foul</span>
  <span m="2449860">on</span> <span m="2450110">you.</span> <span m="2450800">You</span>
  <span m="2451010">shouldn't</span> <span m="2451370">do</span> <span m="2451670">that.</span>
  <span m="2452270">And</span> <span m="2452390">so</span> <span m="2452510">that</span>
  <span m="2452690">means</span> <span m="2452960">I</span> <span m="2454070">can</span>
  <span m="2454190">write</span> <span m="2454340">a</span> <span m="2454400">program</span>
  <span m="2454730">that</span> <span m="2454820">can</span> <span m="2454970">read</span>
  <span m="2455300">this</span> <span m="2455480">data</span> <span m="2455750">really</span>
  <span m="2455990">fast,</span> <span m="2456770">and</span> <span m="2456950">it</span>
  <span m="2457010">can</span> <span m="2457160">write</span> <span m="2457400">this</span>
  <span m="2457880">data</span> <span m="2458150">really</span> <span m="2458390">fast.</span>
  <span m="2458820">And</span> <span m="2458920">that's</span> <span m="2459050">why,</span>
  <span m="2459800">in</span> <span m="2460250">the</span> <span m="2460340">big</span>
  <span m="2460610">data or</span> <span m="2461030">AI</span> <span m="2461360">space,</span>
  <span m="2461960">people</span> <span m="2462290">often</span> <span m="2462590">tend</span>
  <span m="2462830">to</span> <span m="2462950">use</span> <span m="2463490">TSV.</span>
  <span m="2465430">And</span> <span m="2465530">again,</span> <span m="2466040">it's</span>
  <span m="2466280">easily</span> <span m="2466730">readable</span> <span m="2467330">and</span>
  <span m="2467450">writable</span> <span m="2467840">by</span> <span m="2468050">all</span>
  <span m="2468350">those</span> <span m="2468530">spreadsheet</span> <span m="2469040">programs</span>
  <span m="2469640">that</span> <span m="2469820">I</span> <span m="2470030">have</span>
  <span m="2470210">said</span> <span m="2470450">before.</span></p><p><span m="2472250">Databases</span>
  <span m="2473030">play</span> <span m="2473300">a</span> <span m="2473360">very</span>
  <span m="2473630">important</span> <span m="2474050">role</span> <span m="2474440">as</span>
  <span m="2474590">well.</span> <span m="2474890">There's</span> <span m="2475040">several</span>
  <span m="2475400">different</span> <span m="2476360">types</span> <span m="2476720">of</span>
  <span m="2476780">databases</span> <span m="2477830">that</span> <span m="2478280">are</span>
  <span m="2478370">called</span> <span m="2478750">SQL,</span> <span m="2479900">NoSQL,</span>
  <span m="2480650">and</span> <span m="2480720">NewSQL</span> <span m="2480950">.</span>
  <span m="2481790">They're</span> <span m="2482000">good</span> <span m="2482240">for</span>
  <span m="2482450">different</span> <span m="2482810">things.</span> <span m="2483620">I</span>
  <span m="2483770">won't</span> <span m="2484010">dwell</span> <span m="2484370">on</span>
  <span m="2484550">that</span> <span m="2485090">here,</span> <span m="2485600">but</span>
  <span m="2485780">there</span> <span m="2485960">are</span> <span m="2486080">different</span>
  <span m="2486410">types</span> <span m="2486740">of</span> <span m="2486830">databases.</span>
  <span m="2487820">All</span> <span m="2488120">of</span> <span m="2488210">them</span>
  <span m="2488420">operate</span> <span m="2488900">on</span> <span m="2489020">tables.</span>
  <span m="2490670">In</span> <span m="2490790">fact,</span> <span m="2491040">the</span>
  <span m="2491120">central</span> <span m="2491540">object</span> <span m="2492050">in</span>
  <span m="2492230">a</span> <span m="2492350">database</span> <span m="2492800">is</span>
  <span m="2492980">literally</span> <span m="2493340">called</span> <span m="2493670">a</span>
  <span m="2493760">database</span> <span m="2494270">table.</span> <span m="2495230">And</span>
  <span m="2495410">so,</span> <span m="2495790">databases</span> <span m="2496670">play</span>
  <span m="2496910">an</span> <span m="2497000">important</span> <span m="2497390">role.</span>
  <span m="2497720">I</span> <span m="2497780">won't</span> <span m="2497960">go</span>
  <span m="2498080">into</span> <span m="2498230">detail</span> <span m="2498650">here,</span>
  <span m="2499350">but</span> <span m="2499640">I</span> <span m="2499760">just</span>
  <span m="2499910">want</span> <span m="2500150">to</span> <span m="2500270">mention</span>
  <span m="2500600">this.</span></p><p><span m="2501440">Likewise,</span> <span m="2502120">you've</span>
  <span m="2502250">already</span> <span m="2502580">had</span> <span m="2502970">some</span>
  <span m="2503210">demonstrations</span> <span m="2504080">of</span> <span m="2504170">different</span>
  <span m="2504470">languages</span> <span m="2505010">and</span> <span m="2505100">libraries.</span>
  <span m="2505700">I</span> <span m="2505910">think</span> <span m="2506120">everything</span>
  <span m="2506480">you</span> <span m="2506600">saw</span> <span m="2506930">was</span>
  <span m="2507110">in</span> <span m="2507200">Python.</span> <span m="2507860">There's</span>
  <span m="2508040">other</span> <span m="2508250">languages--</span> <span m="2508850">Julia,</span>
  <span m="2509570">MATLAB,</span> <span m="2510350">Octave,</span> <span m="2510940">R--</span>
  <span m="2511700">many</span> <span m="2512000">other</span> <span m="2512180">languages</span>
  <span m="2512750">that</span> <span m="2512870">play</span> <span m="2513080">important</span>
  <span m="2513500">roles</span> <span m="2513890">in</span> <span m="2513980">data</span>
  <span m="2514280">analysis.</span> <span m="2515120">We've</span> <span m="2515270">talked</span>
  <span m="2515540">about</span> <span m="2515720">Jupyter</span> <span m="2516140">Notebooks,</span>
  <span m="2516740">which</span> <span m="2516920">is</span> <span m="2517040">a</span>
  <span m="2517100">universal</span> <span m="2517760">interface</span> <span m="2518690">to</span>
  <span m="2519560">these</span> <span m="2519800">different</span> <span m="2520130">languages</span>
  <span m="2520850">and</span> <span m="2520940">libraries</span> <span m="2521510">to</span>
  <span m="2521600">allow</span> <span m="2521870">you</span> <span m="2521990">to</span>
  <span m="2522110">do</span> <span m="2522320">data</span> <span m="2522620">analysis</span>
  <span m="2523430">in</span> <span m="2523550">addition</span> <span m="2523940">to</span>
  <span m="2524090">the</span> <span m="2524180">various</span> <span m="2525200">machine</span>
  <span m="2525650">learning</span> <span m="2525950">tools.</span> <span m="2526700">We've</span>
  <span m="2526880">talked</span> <span m="2527150">a</span> <span m="2527210">lot</span>
  <span m="2527360">about</span> <span m="2527540">TensorFlow,</span> <span m="2528390">but</span>
  <span m="2528440">there's</span> <span m="2528650">others--</span> <span m="2529130">Theano,</span>
  <span m="2529940">Caffe,</span> <span m="2530600">NVIDEA</span> <span m="2531080">Digits--</span>
  <span m="2531980">all</span> <span m="2532430">are</span> <span m="2533000">examples</span>
  <span m="2533600">of</span> <span m="2533690">different</span> <span m="2534230">tools</span>
  <span m="2534680">for</span> <span m="2534800">doing</span> <span m="2535190">AI.</span>
  <span m="2535940">And</span> <span m="2536030">again,</span> <span m="2536720">they</span>
  <span m="2537290">love</span> <span m="2537740">to</span> <span m="2537890">ingest</span>
  <span m="2538370">tabular</span> <span m="2538850">data,</span> <span m="2539540">and</span>
  <span m="2539690">they're</span> <span m="2539840">very</span> <span m="2540200">good</span>
  <span m="2540650">at</span> <span m="2541160">writing</span> <span m="2541550">out</span>
  <span m="2541820">tabular</span> <span m="2542300">data</span> <span m="2543350">completely</span>
  <span m="2543890">consistent</span> <span m="2544550">with</span> <span m="2545150">that</span>
  <span m="2545390">here.</span></p><p><span m="2546360">And</span> <span m="2546460">then</span>
  <span m="2546530">finally,</span> <span m="2547110">I</span> <span m="2547210">want</span>
  <span m="2547250">to</span> <span m="2547310">mention</span> <span m="2548640">XML</span>
  <span m="2549240">and</span> <span m="2549360">JSON,</span> <span m="2550310">which</span>
  <span m="2550520">are</span> <span m="2550610">very</span> <span m="2550910">popular</span>
  <span m="2551570">in</span> <span m="2551750">object-oriented</span> <span m="2552650">languages,</span>
  <span m="2553730">like</span> <span m="2554390">C++,</span> <span m="2556040">Java,</span>
  <span m="2557060">and</span> <span m="2557210">Python.</span> <span m="2558650">Those</span>
  <span m="2559610">languages</span> <span m="2560270">rely</span> <span m="2561020">on</span>
  <span m="2561680">data</span> <span m="2562010">structures,</span> <span m="2563790">which</span>
  <span m="2564200">are</span> <span m="2564290">basically</span> <span m="2564830">just</span>
  <span m="2565220">a</span> <span m="2565280">set</span> <span m="2565700">of</span>
  <span m="2566090">fields,</span> <span m="2567050">and</span> <span m="2567200">then</span>
  <span m="2567410">those</span> <span m="2567740">fields</span> <span m="2568130">can</span>
  <span m="2568310">also</span> <span m="2568760">be</span> <span m="2569000">data</span>
  <span m="2569300">structures,</span> <span m="2569900">and</span> <span m="2569990">this</span>
  <span m="2570170">can</span> <span m="2570350">continue</span> <span m="2570960">on.</span>
  <span m="2571190">These</span> <span m="2571370">are</span> <span m="2571460">called</span>
  <span m="2571700">hierarchical</span> <span m="2572540">data</span> <span m="2572810">structures,</span>
  <span m="2573890">the</span> <span m="2574010">way</span> <span m="2574700">these</span>
  <span m="2574880">languages</span> <span m="2575420">are</span> <span m="2575540">organized.</span></p><p><span
  m="2576540">And</span> <span m="2576560">so</span> <span m="2576710">it's</span>
  <span m="2576830">very</span> <span m="2577100">natural</span> <span m="2577580">for</span>
  <span m="2577700">them</span> <span m="2577880">to</span> <span m="2578000">have</span>
  <span m="2578150">formats</span> <span m="2579080">that</span> <span m="2579320">they</span>
  <span m="2579500">can</span> <span m="2579650">just</span> <span m="2579800">say,</span>
  <span m="2579980">write</span> <span m="2580310">out</span> <span m="2580490">this</span>
  <span m="2581150">whole</span> <span m="2581420">blob</span> <span m="2581780">of</span>
  <span m="2581900">data,</span> <span m="2582560">and</span> <span m="2582680">it
  will</span> <span m="2582830">write</span> <span m="2583070">it</span> <span m="2583190">out</span>
  <span m="2583370">into</span> <span m="2583610">a</span> <span m="2583670">hierarchical</span>
  <span m="2584360">form</span> <span m="2585050">called</span> <span m="2585350">XML</span>
  <span m="2586010">or</span> <span m="2586130">JSON.</span> <span m="2587300">However,</span>
  <span m="2588230">it's</span> <span m="2588410">not</span> <span m="2588680">very</span>
  <span m="2588980">human</span> <span m="2589280">readable.</span> <span m="2590990">And</span>
  <span m="2591800">I</span> <span m="2591920">just</span> <span m="2592160">told</span>
  <span m="2592640">you</span> <span m="2593120">that</span> <span m="2593270">all</span>
  <span m="2593480">the</span> <span m="2593600">data</span> <span m="2593840">analysis</span>
  <span m="2594380">tools</span> <span m="2594680">want</span> <span m="2594950">tables,</span>
  <span m="2595890">which</span> <span m="2596000">means</span> <span m="2596630">that</span>
  <span m="2596780">these</span> <span m="2597020">formats</span> <span m="2597640">aren't</span>
  <span m="2598040">necessarily</span> <span m="2598760">very</span> <span m="2599060">good</span>
  <span m="2599630">for</span> <span m="2599810">doing</span> <span m="2600680">data</span>
  <span m="2600950">analysis</span> <span m="2601220">on.</span></p><p><span m="2602060">Fortunately,</span>
  <span m="2602750">we've</span> <span m="2602960">discovered</span> <span m="2603500">some</span>
  <span m="2603770">ways</span> <span m="2604520">that</span> <span m="2604670">we</span>
  <span m="2604850">can</span> <span m="2605030">basically</span> <span m="2605630">convert</span>
  <span m="2607010">these</span> <span m="2607220">hierarchical</span> <span m="2607820">formats</span>
  <span m="2608600">into</span> <span m="2608930">a</span> <span m="2609020">giant,</span>
  <span m="2609350">what</span> <span m="2609470">we</span> <span m="2609590">call,</span>
  <span m="2609830">sparse</span> <span m="2610280">table.</span> <span m="2611540">And</span>
  <span m="2612200">sparse</span> <span m="2612680">just</span> <span m="2612950">means</span>
  <span m="2613280">a</span> <span m="2613340">table</span> <span m="2614030">where</span>
  <span m="2614180">lots</span> <span m="2614570">of</span> <span m="2614640">the</span>
  <span m="2614780">values</span> <span m="2615260">are</span> <span m="2617270">empty.</span>
  <span m="2618470">The</span> <span m="2618590">entries</span> <span m="2619070">are</span>
  <span m="2619220">empty.</span> <span m="2620280">And</span> <span m="2620480">so</span>
  <span m="2621200">we</span> <span m="2621350">can</span> <span m="2621500">just</span>
  <span m="2621680">use</span> <span m="2621920">that</span> <span m="2622160">space</span>
  <span m="2622610">to</span> <span m="2622730">represent</span> <span m="2623300">this</span>
  <span m="2623450">hierarchy,</span> <span m="2624410">and</span> <span m="2624650">all</span>
  <span m="2624980">the</span> <span m="2625100">tools</span> <span m="2625490">we've</span>
  <span m="2625640">just</span> <span m="2625850">talked</span> <span m="2626210">about</span>
  <span m="2626710">can</span> <span m="2626960">ingest</span> <span m="2627380">this</span>
  <span m="2627590">data</span> <span m="2628100">pretty</span> <span m="2628430">easily.</span></p><p><span
  m="2631180">Because</span> <span m="2631660">tables</span> <span m="2632170">are</span>
  <span m="2632320">so</span> <span m="2632530">popular,</span> <span m="2634360">every</span>
  <span m="2634720">single</span> <span m="2636640">different</span> <span m="2637090">approach</span>
  <span m="2637720">or</span> <span m="2637840">software</span> <span m="2638380">package--</span>
  <span m="2638980">and</span> <span m="2639080">we</span> <span m="2639190">have</span>
  <span m="2639340">a</span> <span m="2639430">bunch</span> <span m="2639820">of</span>
  <span m="2639880">them</span> <span m="2640070">listed</span> <span m="2640780">in</span>
  <span m="2641700">the</span> <span m="2641800">first</span> <span m="2642130">column,</span>
  <span m="2642550">here--</span> <span m="2644020">assign</span> <span m="2644470">different</span>
  <span m="2644890">names</span> <span m="2645400">to</span> <span m="2645640">the</span>
  <span m="2645760">standard</span> <span m="2646630">ways</span> <span m="2647080">we</span>
  <span m="2647230">refer</span> <span m="2647740">to</span> <span m="2648580">the</span>
  <span m="2648730">elements</span> <span m="2649210">of</span> <span m="2649300">a</span>
  <span m="2649360">table.</span> <span m="2650170">And</span> <span m="2650290">there</span>
  <span m="2650440">aren't</span> <span m="2650710">that</span> <span m="2650950">many.</span>
  <span m="2651440">So</span> <span m="2651520">when</span> <span m="2651670">you</span>
  <span m="2651760">think</span> <span m="2652000">about</span> <span m="2652210">a</span>
  <span m="2652270">table,</span> <span m="2652720">there's</span> <span m="2652870">certain</span>
  <span m="2653200">standard</span> <span m="2654130">terms</span> <span m="2654730">for</span>
  <span m="2654940">dealing</span> <span m="2655330">with</span> <span m="2655840">what</span>
  <span m="2655990">do</span> <span m="2656080">we</span> <span m="2656170">call</span>
  <span m="2656530">the</span> <span m="2656650">table?</span> <span m="2657640">In</span>
  <span m="2657760">Excel</span> <span m="2658270">it's</span> <span m="2658420">called</span>
  <span m="2658660">a</span> <span m="2658720">sheet.</span> <span m="2661660">How</span>
  <span m="2662200">do</span> <span m="2662260">we</span> <span m="2662470">refer</span>
  <span m="2662890">to</span> <span m="2663070">a</span> <span m="2663130">particular</span>
  <span m="2663670">row?</span> <span m="2664570">What</span> <span m="2664720">do</span>
  <span m="2664780">we</span> <span m="2664900">call</span> <span m="2665200">a</span>
  <span m="2665260">whole</span> <span m="2665830">row?</span> <span m="2666550">How</span>
  <span m="2666760">do</span> <span m="2666850">we</span> <span m="2667240">refer</span>
  <span m="2667660">to</span> <span m="2667870">a</span> <span m="2667930">particular</span>
  <span m="2668410">column?</span> <span m="2669160">What</span> <span m="2669310">do</span>
  <span m="2669370">we</span> <span m="2669490">call</span> <span m="2670080">a</span>
  <span m="2670150">whole</span> <span m="2670390">column?</span> <span m="2671260">What</span>
  <span m="2671410">do</span> <span m="2671470">we</span> <span m="2671590">call</span>
  <span m="2671980">an</span> <span m="2672190">entry?</span> <span m="2673030">And</span>
  <span m="2673180">what</span> <span m="2673360">kind</span> <span m="2673600">of</span>
  <span m="2673690">math</span> <span m="2674050">can</span> <span m="2674260">we</span>
  <span m="2674380">do</span> <span m="2674680">on</span> <span m="2674830">it?</span></p><p><span
  m="2675530">And</span> <span m="2675580">so,</span> <span m="2675790">whenever</span>
  <span m="2676300">you're</span> <span m="2676540">encountering</span> <span m="2677620">a</span>
  <span m="2677710">new</span> <span m="2677950">piece</span> <span m="2678250">of</span>
  <span m="2678370">software--</span> <span m="2678970">And</span> <span m="2679090">we</span>
  <span m="2679390">deal</span> <span m="2679660">with</span> <span m="2679840">it</span>
  <span m="2679930">all</span> <span m="2680110">the</span> <span m="2680230">time,</span>
  <span m="2680590">but a</span> <span m="2680620">lot</span> <span m="2680860">of</span>
  <span m="2680920">times</span> <span m="2681160">you'll</span> <span m="2681280">get</span>
  <span m="2681550">software,</span> <span m="2682360">and</span> <span m="2682450">maybe</span>
  <span m="2682690">it's</span> <span m="2682840">related</span> <span m="2683230">to</span>
  <span m="2683350">data</span> <span m="2683620">analysis</span> <span m="2684100">seems</span>
  <span m="2684460">really,</span> <span m="2684890">really</span> <span m="2685030">confusing.</span>
  <span m="2686540">It's</span> <span m="2686620">probably</span> <span m="2687250">working</span>
  <span m="2687640">on</span> <span m="2687760">tables,</span> <span m="2688270">and</span>
  <span m="2688390">so</span> <span m="2688600">all</span> <span m="2688810">you</span>
  <span m="2688960">have</span> <span m="2689170">to</span> <span m="2689320">need</span>
  <span m="2689740">to</span> <span m="2689920">learn</span> <span m="2690310">is</span>
  <span m="2690730">what</span> <span m="2690940">are</span> <span m="2691000">they</span>
  <span m="2691150">calling</span> <span m="2691600">these</span> <span m="2691930">things.</span>
  <span m="2693320">And</span> <span m="2693520">different</span> <span m="2694000">software</span>
  <span m="2694630">gives it</span> <span m="2694990">different</span> <span m="2695410">names,</span>
  <span m="2695800">just</span> <span m="2696040">for</span> <span m="2696520">arbitrary</span>
  <span m="2697210">historical</span> <span m="2697840">reasons.</span> <span m="2698830">And</span>
  <span m="2699010">so,</span> <span m="2699700">if</span> <span m="2699820">you</span>
  <span m="2699940">can</span> <span m="2700060">figure</span> <span m="2700480">out</span>
  <span m="2700690">what</span> <span m="2701470">it's</span> <span m="2701680">calling</span>
  <span m="2702070">these</span> <span m="2702400">things,</span> <span m="2703060">then</span>
  <span m="2703270">you'll</span> <span m="2703420">discover</span> <span m="2704170">the</span>
  <span m="2704260">software</span> <span m="2704630">is</span> <span m="2704830">a</span>
  <span m="2704890">lot</span> <span m="2705190">easier</span> <span m="2705490">to</span>
  <span m="2705610">understand.</span> <span m="2706610">So</span> <span m="2706810">we</span>
  <span m="2706930">definitely</span> <span m="2707380">encourage</span> <span m="2707860">you</span>
  <span m="2708010">to</span> <span m="2708880">just</span> <span m="2709420">map</span>
  <span m="2709900">whatever</span> <span m="2710230">software</span> <span m="2710740">into</span>
  <span m="2711010">these</span> <span m="2711250">concepts,</span> <span m="2711910">and</span>
  <span m="2712030">all</span> <span m="2712210">of</span> <span m="2712270">sudden</span>
  <span m="2712570">life</span> <span m="2712810">becomes</span> <span m="2713170">a</span>
  <span m="2713230">lot</span> <span m="2713470">easier.</span></p><p><span m="2715970">And</span>
  <span m="2716140">because</span> <span m="2716890">tabular</span> <span m="2717400">data</span>
  <span m="2717730">is</span> <span m="2717910">used</span> <span m="2718750">so</span>
  <span m="2719170">commonly,</span> <span m="2720070">whether</span> <span m="2720260">it</span>
  <span m="2720340">be in</span> <span m="2720520">spreadsheets</span> <span m="2721240">or</span>
  <span m="2721330">analyzing</span> <span m="2721810">graphs</span> <span m="2722290">or</span>
  <span m="2722350">databases</span> <span m="2723070">or</span> <span m="2723160">matrices,</span>
  <span m="2724120">it's</span> <span m="2724300">a</span> <span m="2724360">natural</span>
  <span m="2724870">interchange</span> <span m="2725380">format.</span> <span m="2726190">So</span>
  <span m="2726820">by</span> <span m="2727870">reading</span> <span m="2728290">in</span>
  <span m="2728380">tabular</span> <span m="2728860">data</span> <span m="2729430">and</span>
  <span m="2729580">writing</span> <span m="2730030">out</span> <span m="2730150">tabular</span>
  <span m="2730600">data,</span> <span m="2730930">you're</span> <span m="2731110">preserving</span>
  <span m="2731680">your</span> <span m="2731800">ability</span> <span m="2732520">to</span>
  <span m="2732910">have</span> <span m="2733930">that</span> <span m="2734170">data</span>
  <span m="2734530">go</span> <span m="2734800">into</span> <span m="2735040">any</span>
  <span m="2735340">application.</span> <span m="2736390">Again,</span> <span m="2736690">you</span>
  <span m="2736810">have</span> <span m="2736990">to</span> <span m="2737080">be</span>
  <span m="2737200">careful</span> <span m="2737650">about</span> <span m="2737890">people</span>
  <span m="2738250">who</span> <span m="2738370">want</span> <span m="2738670">to</span>
  <span m="2738820">write</span> <span m="2739060">proprietary</span> <span m="2739810">formats</span>
  <span m="2740740">because</span> <span m="2741100">they're</span> <span m="2741220">basically,</span>
  <span m="2741900">sort of,</span> <span m="2742300">preventing</span> <span m="2742900">you</span>
  <span m="2743230">from</span> <span m="2744190">basically</span> <span m="2744910">working</span>
  <span m="2745420">with</span> <span m="2745630">other</span> <span m="2745870">tools</span>
  <span m="2746380">and</span> <span m="2746470">other</span> <span m="2746710">communities.</span>
  <span m="2747310">And</span> <span m="2747400">this</span> <span m="2747580">is</span>
  <span m="2747700">another</span> <span m="2747970">reason</span> <span m="2748240">why</span>
  <span m="2748360">tabular</span> <span m="2748720">data</span> <span m="2749020">is</span>
  <span m="2749140">so</span> <span m="2749380">great.</span></p><p><span m="2751440">All</span>
  <span m="2751500">right,</span> <span m="2751630">so</span> <span m="2751750">moving</span>
  <span m="2752140">on</span> <span m="2752380">here,</span> <span m="2752620">I</span>
  <span m="2752680">wanted</span> <span m="2752890">to just</span> <span m="2752980">talk</span>

  <span m="2944420">a</span> <span m="2944450">very</span> <span m="2944750">good</span>

  <span m="2955850">not</span> <span m="2956180">work</span> <span m="2956600">with</span>
  <span m="2956840">small</span> <span m="2957350">files</span> <span m="2957890">really</span>
  <span m="2958190">well.</span> <span m="2959540">You</span> <span m="2959690">do</span>
  <span m="2959960">want</span> <span m="2960140">to</span> <span m="2960230">compress.</span>
  <span m="2961670">Decompression</span> <span m="2962540">doesn't</span> <span m="2962900">take</span>
  <span m="2963230">much</span> <span m="2963500">time.</span> <span m="2964370">It's</span>
  <span m="2964580">usually</span> <span m="2964940">quite</span> <span m="2965240">beneficial.</span>
  <span m="2966570">And</span> <span m="2966650">so,</span> <span m="2966890">it's</span>
  <span m="2967010">better</span> <span m="2967250">to</span> <span m="2967340">have</span>
  <span m="2967640">fewer</span> <span m="2968000">larger</span> <span m="2968450">files.</span>
  <span m="2970180">A</span> <span m="2970280">sweet</span> <span m="2970610">spot,</span>
  <span m="2970970">for</span> <span m="2971180">a</span> <span m="2971240">long</span>

  <span m="2972350">file</span> <span m="2972760">serving</span> <span m="2973130">the</span>
